		# ===================== 清理修正 =====================
		NPC = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						not = { check_variable = { which = quanguorenkou value = 1 } }
						check_variable = { which = quanguorenkou value = 2 }
					}
				}
				any_owned = { remove_province_modifier = quanguorenkou_1 }
			}
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						not = { check_variable = { which = quanguorenkou value = 2 } }
